this is an attack on the global commons .	這是對全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要考慮如何處理
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	來轉換到另一種海洋 , 網路海
here are photographs of two young men .	這裡有兩位年輕男士的照片
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	在當下 , 他們被監禁 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們做了一個信用卡詐欺案 , 讓他們淨利超過100億美元 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 這是全球經濟的2兆年不連續性 。
two trillion a year .	一年有兩兆
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	那只是在英國的國內生產毛額下 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以這個網路大海 , 我們無止境地知道 , 是徹底開放的基本一部分 , 也受到了威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	我擔心全球公有物的另一件事 , 就是被販賣所造成的威脅 , 被毒品、鴉片的運動所影響 , 來自阿富汗 , 透過歐洲到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心來自安地斯山脊北邊的可卡因 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器和人口販賣的運動 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的可怕成本 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	人口販賣主要在海上移動 , 但在全球公有物的其他地方 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴你們這是我們海軍裝備的高科技作品我們用它來阻止販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是由毒品卡特爾所執行的半機械人 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	在南美的叢林裡建造
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那個低科技的木筏抓到它 , 它帶著六噸的古柯鹼 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個船員 。 精密的溝通
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣 , 在毒品中 , 在人類身上 , 在武器上 , 上帝禁止 , 在大規模毀滅性的武器中 , 是對全球公有物的威脅之一 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	今天我們一起在阿富汗
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是阿富汗的一塊花花田 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世界上百分之八十到九十的辣椒、鴉片和海洛因 , 從阿富汗出來 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	我們也看到那裡 , 當然 , 恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是蓋達組織從這裡開始的 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個非常強烈的迫切性嵌在那裡 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的關注也是全球公有物的一部分 , 以及我們必須處理的是什麼 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以在這裡 , 21世紀
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們20世紀的工具是行不通的 。
what should we do ?	我們應該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我會主張 , 我們不會一桶一桶一桶一桶一桶一桶的安全遞送 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不會一桶一桶一桶一桶一桶的槍 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這樣做時 , 我們必須做得很好 , 且要有能力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關於國際、跨國、私人的連結 , 由這個在網路上策略性溝通的概念拉在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這如何用正面的方式
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 , 這些是阿富汗士兵
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 這很奇怪 。 我以為我讀到 , 這種人口、年輕男女 , 在20、30歲時 , 大多在阿富汗是不識字的 。 」
you would be correct .	你會是正確的
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 , 85%無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班的教育期間這些男人和女人都會學會閱讀
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿著書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們在文字課程中讀書 , 由nato和私營機構合作 , 和發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教導了超過二十萬阿富汗的安全力量 , 以基本的層面來看待和寫作 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你能在阿富汗讀和寫時 , 你通常會在口袋裡放一支筆 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在儀式上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們帶著那枝筆 , 帶著很棒的驕傲 , 放在他們的口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這將國際間的50個國家集結起來 , 參與這項任務 , 跨國的50個國家──這些發展機構──以及私人公開 , 來採取這種安全措施 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教他們戰鬥技能 , 但我會主張 , 開放資源安全意味著用更長的保安方式來連結 , 創造更長的保障效應 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	叫做舒適感 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有個姐姐船名叫mercy ,
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船隻 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這一個 , 舒適感 , 在加勒比海和南美海岸進行病人治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在典型的十字架上 , 他們會進行四十萬個病人的治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它不是被軍隊嚴格的 , 而是結合人道主義組織:營運希望、計畫微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織發送志工
interagency physicians come out .	國際醫師出櫃
they're all part of this .	他們都是這方面的一部分
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子來說明這可能會有的影響 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 帶著他的母親走了兩天 , 來到舒適的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他符合時 , 在他極度神話的眼中 , 他突然向上望 , 說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽媽 , 我看到了世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	把這個乘以40萬個病人治療 , 這個私人的合作與安全力量合作 , 你開始看到創造安全的力量 , 以非常不同的方式創造安全的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	在這裡你看到棒球選手
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在這張照片中挑出兩位美國軍人嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這些年輕男孩的兩位年輕男生 。 這是一連串棒球診所的一部分 , 我們在大聯盟棒球場和加勒比大聯盟之間的合作 , 他們建立了國務院的外交部門 , 軍隊棒球選手 , 他們是真正有技能的士兵 , 但參與了這個任務 , 他們在拉丁美洲和加勒比海 , 和加勒比海 , 和加勒比海 , 在加拉加拉瓜 , 創造了全美洲的診所 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕男性和女性展現了典範 , 關於健身以及生活的典範 , 我主張協助為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這夥伴關係的另一個面向是在災難的解脫中 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是一台美國空軍直升機在2004年海嘯之後參與 , 殺害了25萬人 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在每一個重大災難中2004年海嘯 , 25萬人死亡 , 2005年巴基斯坦的喀什米里地震 , 2005年 , 8萬5千人死亡 , 海地地震 , 大約30萬人死亡 , 更近期是嚴重的地震綜合了日本和其核子產業的結合 。 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際事業之間的合作關係 , 國際事務所 , 國際事務所 , 私有的合作關係 , 和安全合作 , 和安全的合作關係 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	所以這些例子都是開源安全的概念 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們把它綁在一起 , 漸漸地 , 藉由這樣做 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看到的是這種思維: 「 啊 , 老實說吧 , 這些一定是溝通的海道 , 或這些可能是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不是的 。 這是根據twitter的世界的圖表 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 。 綠色是地緣分配 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成的 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是一場很棒的人口調查的完美演化 , 世界上六大國家都以下降順序:中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們想在這些蚊帳裡
why do we want to be involved ?	為什麼我們要參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們先前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉另一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦演講過一陣子 。 我說 , 如同我對你們所有人說的 , 我在臉書上 。 朋友我 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	收到觀眾的笑聲
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有篇文章是由ap , 在電線上運行 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	在世界上兩個地方被撿起來:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北約熱門需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上我有數百個臉書朋友 , 來自印尼人和芬蘭人 , 大部分會說: 「 承認吧 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 噢 , 順便說 , nato是什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	沒錯 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何移動訊息 , 移動那個訊息的方式 , 就是我們如何連結國際、國際、私人、和這些社會網 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我打一個十一月的筆記 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭警衛隊裡
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在希爾曼蘭的手錶 , 在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡來提醒我們 , 我不想讓任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要能力 , 能夠創造真正的軍事效果 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這就是我們是誰的核心 , 我們所做的 , 我們要保護自由 , 言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍藏的東西 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道的 , 人生並不是一個開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有一支軍隊 , 要麼在艱難的戰鬥中 , 要麼就在牢牢裡 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會主張生命是無私的 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你得把它撥進去 , 正如我所想 , 我們在這21世紀是如何創造安全的 , 會有時候 , 我們會在真正的戰爭和危機中施加艱難的力量 , 但會有許多例子 , 如今日我們所談過的 , 我們的軍隊可以成為創造21世紀安全的一部分 , 國際安全 , 國際 , 國際間 , 私人交流 , 和競爭的溝通連結 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我要說我們今天早期聽到維基百科 。 我常常用維基百科來查證事實 , 正如你們所有人所欣賞的 , 維基百科並不是由12位傑出的人所創立的 , 鎖定在一間房間寫文章的房間裡 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天都有成千上萬的人在輸入資訊 , 每天有數百萬人會退縮這些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	對於我們所有人一起思考的基本點 , 這是個完美的圖像 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個盟友 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有一個人 , 就跟我們所有人一起思考一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基的願景是非常簡單的:一個每個人可以自由分享的世界 , 在所有知識的總和中 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 透過結合國際、跨國、私人、策略性溝通 , 在這個21世紀 , 我們就能創造出所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常感謝 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。
